## Skipped Tests

799 tests were skipped.

<details>
<summary>Click to expand</summary>

- `parallel/test-aborted-util.js`: requires --expose-internals and internal/abort_controller
- `parallel/test-abortsignal-cloneable.js`: requires transferableAbortController and MessageChannel
- `parallel/test-assert-async.js`: assert.rejects does not set generatedMessage:true when rejection doesn't match; pre-existing issue
- `parallel/test-assert-builtins-not-read-from-filesystem.js`: requires child_process.spawnSync which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-assert-checktag.js`: QuickJS globalThis/process lack V8 internal type tags; notDeepEqual cannot distinguish faked copies
- `parallel/test-assert-deep.js`: notDeepEqual/notDeepStrictEqual fails on some edge cases (missing exception for equivalent boxed primitives)
- `parallel/test-assert-esm-cjs-message-verify.js`: requires process spawning (spawnPromisified) which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-assert-first-line.js`: requires loading fixture files from filesystem which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-assert-objects.js`: partialDeepStrictEqual tests cause WASM stack overflow due to deep recursion exceeding WASM stack limits
- `parallel/test-assert.js`: requires source-code inspection (reading call-site expressions for assert.ok falsy messages) which is not available in QuickJS/WASM
- `parallel/test-async-hooks-execution-async-resource-await.js`: requires HTTP server functionality, we only support clients
- `parallel/test-async-hooks-execution-async-resource.js`: requires HTTP server functionality, we only support clients
- `parallel/test-async-hooks-http-parser-destroy.js`: requires HTTP server functionality, we only support clients
- `parallel/test-buffer-alloc.js`: QuickJS Uint8Array error message format differs from V8 for new Uint8Array(kMaxLength+1)
- `parallel/test-buffer-arraybuffer.js`: QuickJS prototype chain for fake ArrayBuffer subclass differs from V8 (AB constructor without super() still passes instanceof)
- `parallel/test-buffer-constants.js`: QuickJS kStringMaxLength differs from V8; string repeat at 256MB may OOM instead of throwing RangeError
- `parallel/test-buffer-inspect.js`: requires util.inspect integration to show custom properties on Buffer instances
- `parallel/test-buffer-pool-untransferable.js`: requires worker_threads MessageChannel which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-buffer-tostring-range.js`: common.skipIf32Bits() call errors due to require.main.filename being undefined in WASM environment
- `parallel/test-buffer-write.js`: requires internal asciiWrite/latin1Write/utf8Write prototype methods with bounds checking
- `parallel/test-child-process-advanced-serialization-largebuffer.js`: requires child_process which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-child-process-advanced-serialization-splitted-length-field.js`: requires child_process which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-child-process-advanced-serialization.js`: requires child_process which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-child-process-can-write-to-stdout.js`: requires child_process which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-child-process-constructor.js`: requires child_process which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-child-process-cwd.js`: requires child_process which is not available in WASM
- `parallel/test-child-process-default-options.js`: requires child_process which is not available in WASM
